  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText3076625657276631319" style="display:none">***Author Note: This is not a love story. This is a story of love gone wrong.***<br /><br />Growing up the way I did, you’d think I’d be more screwed up than what I actually am.<br /><br />Soon as I turned sixteen, I left that bump in the road I called home and took my chances on the street.<br /><br />Best decision I ever made.<br /><br />Now, at the age of twenty six, I’m educated, employed and damn good at my job.<br /><br />My friends have become my family. Like me, they know what it’s like to grow up unloved.<br /><br />But the saying is true.<br /><br />The world makes way for those who know where they are going.<br /><br />That’s me.<br /><br />I know where I’m going and I’ll get there eventually. On my own terms and at my own pace.<br /><br />But then there’s him.<br /><br />I feel his eyes on me. I see him hiding in plain sight. He watches me.<br /><br />He makes me feel.<br /><br />It’s unconventional.<br /><br />But it’s real.<br /><br />I’m sure you’re wondering how a person falls in love with their stalker.<br /><br />So am I.<br /><br />This isn’t a story.<br /><br />This is my life.</span>

<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">The second book apparently is about two different people, named Alejandra Gambino and Julius Carter. It hasn't been released yet, and the publishing d<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">The second book apparently is about two different people, named Alejandra Gambino and Julius Carter. It hasn't been released yet, and the publishing date has already passed and has not been updated, so I recommend you don't get your hopes up for a continuation of this story. Here's the link: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21403041-dirty">https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2...</a><br />But... In the series, there's also another book, that is not published as well, titled Raw: Rebirth (The to-be 3rd book of the series) which may imply to a continuation. But take my advice: Don't get your hopes up. <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24704846-raw">https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2...</a><a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer870301914" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11226752351915373700">I think I saw this story on an episode of <i>Law & Order: Special Victims Unit</i>.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393870170i/8775167.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/><b>
  <i>"Just as I’m about to give up, I see him. He watches me from under the hood of his jacket, reclining on a café chair. I know I should report this. He’s everywhere. And I mean everywhere. It almost seems like he knows where I’m going to be before I know."</i>
</b><br/><br/>I swear I wasn't going to review this book. I'm actually reading a bunch of "dark" romance/erotica books as part of a project with my college book society - we're</span>
  <span id="freeText11226752351915373700" style="display:none">I think I saw this story on an episode of <i>Law &amp; Order: Special Victims Unit</i>.<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393870170i/8775167.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><b>
  <i>"Just as I’m about to give up, I see him. He watches me from under the hood of his jacket, reclining on a café chair. I know I should report this. He’s everywhere. And I mean everywhere. It almost seems like he knows where I’m going to be before I know."</i>
</b><br><br>I swear I wasn't going to review this book. I'm actually reading a bunch of "dark" romance/erotica books as part of a project with my college book society - we're critically examining the recent influx of these in the indie publishing world, particularly the way women are portrayed in them. And I wasn't going to review them because I knew I would probably hate them and no one wants to read review after review of negativity. I knew what I was letting myself in for and I knew it wasn't my thing. But... then this book happened.<br><br>Here's the funny thing: I wasn't put off by all the dark sexy stuff and questionable behaviour. I wasn't put off by Twitch's (yeah, that's his name) need to "break" Lexi. I wasn't even put off when he compared her to a dog or when he carried out his psycho-stalkery crap. I expected all of that. I got it - he's a villain and we're not supposed to like him. 'kay, whatever. What did it for me - and what made me want to review this book despite everything I've said - was Lexi's stupid, <b>stupid fucking behaviour</b>. A few other things too, but mostly that.<br><br><i>
  <b>"Once we reach my unit and he opens the door, it doesn’t hit me until we’re inside that he knows where I live. <br>So why don’t you feel like you’re in danger? <br>Because I’m not. I just know it. I’m sure of it."</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393874298i/8775910._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And: <b>
  <i>"Not sure why I’m taking orders from a man who likes to watch me from under a hood, but I am."</i>
</b> Refer to image above^.<br><br>I don't know how I made it through all the stupid in this book, I seriously don't. On top of all the "whisper-yelling" and "whisper-hissing" which is the only way people talk in this novel, and the endless amount of filler sex where Lexi waxes poetic about Twitch's beautiful dick. Ugh. My favourite (read: hated it) thing is that the first "message" this novel delivers is that stalkery behaviour can be a good thing. In chapter one, Twitch swoops in to rescue Lexi from a would-be rapist:<br><br><b>
  <i>I whisper, “I just want to know why you watch me?”<br>Not answering, he states acidly, “It was a fucking good thing I was, don’t you think?”<br>An awkward, foul silence follows.</i>
</b><br><br>No!! It wasn't a good thing, you crazy ass piece of shit. This crap happens in <i>Fifty Shades of Grey</i> too, as well as other books. The guy acts like a douchebag/stalker/control freak and his behaviour happens to save the heroine from some tragedy or other and this is used to <u>excuse said behaviour</u>. What if a guy punches you in the face and accidentally knocks you out of the path of a speeding bus? Does that make him a hero?<br><br>Pg 22. <b>
  <i>"It’s strange. He doesn’t look like a predator. Certainly doesn’t act like one. So what’s the deal?</i>
</b><br><br>1) <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393875589i/8776093._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>"Hello there, I'm Joseph Stalin, nice to meet you! Please make yourself at home. Can I get you anything? Some tea or coffee, perhaps? <u>Oh, and by the way, I'm responsible for the deaths of somewhere between 20 and 60 million people.</u>"<br><br>He doesn't look like a predator? <b>They never fucking do</b>. That's why they're so good at it. If ugly men were staring at you from the shadows, you'd be dragging your stupid ass down to the police station, am I right?<br><br>2) <b>He doesn't act like one?</b> He stalks you. He knows your name and where you live without ever having spoken to you. Lexi, I'd hate to see your idea of a predator.<br><br>Oh yeah, and... <b>
  <i>My brain interrupts me with, “You do realize you just had crazy-assed sex with a homeless, crazy-assed stalker-dude, right? You also let this guy come inside you and you’ve known him about a minute and a half.”</i>
</b><br><br>Without any protection, I might add. She lets her stalker into her house, has sex with him, and doesn't even use a condom.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393876192ra/8776188.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lexi is a particular brand of moron that appears a lot in romance novels. Not only is she ridiculously stupid, but we are supposed to believe she is special. A good girl. Intelligent. Kind. Caring. Above other "slutty" women. SO SPESHUL. She can't even dress as Cleopatra for fancy dress because she's too damn nice:<br><br><b>
  <i>“No, babe. You’re not Cleopatra. You’re an angel. And a beautiful one at that.”</i>
</b><br><br>When she visits Twitch at work, she immediately hates the beautiful woman who works for him: <b>
  <i>"Her perfect red-stained lips match her perfect... everything. I dislike this woman very muchly."</i>
</b><br><br>Also, I wanted to mention something else about this. I am a white woman living in Britain so I don't really have any concept of racism myself. I've seen it around me on occasion in all its ugliness, but it has never been directed at me and I won't pretend to know what it's like. So maybe I'm reading too much into this... but I felt extremely uncomfortable when Lexi scornfully refers to Ling as "Miss Asia". Maybe it is because Ling is treated as disposable and with disdain by everybody in this book. She is called everything from whore to skank to bitch and brushed aside by Twitch like she has no feelings whatsoever. Everything about her characterization didn't sit right with me.<br><br>There are so many more quotes I could pull up for you, but I think you'll have probably worked out by now whether you can stomach this book or not. In terms of plot, it is mostly sex. With a nice big side order of angst. I also predicted the ending fairly early and I thought the "reveals" for Twitch's stalkery were ridiculous. His explanation didn't really make sense and wasn't particularly convincing. Oh well, what did I expect?<br><br>Here's one final quote to sum up the wonderful man that Twitch is: <b>
  <i>"You start this and change your mind, I won’t stop."</i>
</b><br><br>You know what it is if someone refuses to stop when you change your mind during sex? Of course you do, you're not stupid. You're not Lexi.<br><br><a href="http://thebookgeek.co.uk" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.leafmarks.com/emilymay" rel="nofollow noopener">Leafmarks</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/thebookgeekreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/thebookgeek01" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://instagram.com/emleemay" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="http://mycountryheart.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11226752351915373700" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_740258810" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/740258810" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/740258810?book_show_action=true">Oct 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940148861119" href="/book/show/18468559-raw">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">sex with no plot lovers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=bdsm">bdsm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=douchenugget">douchenugget</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=panty-dropping-hot">panty-dropping-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=oops-let-s-do-it-again-romance">oops-let-s-do-it-again-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=read-to-review">read-to-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=contemporary-duckie">contemporary-duckie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=love-hate-swingaroo">love-hate-swingaroo</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=alpha-heroes">alpha-heroes</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer740258810" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15183359282164642176"><b>2 stars</b><br/><br/>Being honest sucks donkey balls. Okay I'm going to cut the sweet talk and just list what I didn't like.<br/><br/><b>Numero Uno:</b> Writing style<br/><br/>There are some books that have the perfect plot, amazing characters, and dynamic chemistry, but I still don’t like. Why? If I can’t even <i>read</i> the book because of the way it’s styled, then I <i>just can’t read the book.</i> It’s not that the author’s style was <u>bad,</u> no. It’s just for <i>me</i> I can’t stand all the fuckin’, darlin’, and other words missing the <b>“g”</b> key, along wit</span>
  <span id="freeText15183359282164642176" style="display:none"><b>2 stars</b><br /><br />Being honest sucks donkey balls. Okay I'm going to cut the sweet talk and just list what I didn't like.<br /><br /><b>Numero Uno:</b> Writing style<br /><br />There are some books that have the perfect plot, amazing characters, and dynamic chemistry, but I still don’t like. Why? If I can’t even <i>read</i> the book because of the way it’s styled, then I <i>just can’t read the book.</i> It’s not that the author’s style was <u>bad,</u> no. It’s just for <i>me</i> I can’t stand all the fuckin’, darlin’, and other words missing the <b>“g”</b> key, along with chopped up sentences like “You just gotta.” &lt;--- I just got to what? <br /><br />What else was bothersome? The endearments. 81 instances of ‘babe’ and ‘angel.’ I also don’t like it when all the characters address each other as babe. I know, I know. It’s a way of conveying affection but for hardcore readers like myself, it symbolizes way too much mush, not enough grit. That may just be a personal preference, or I just don’t roll with Aussie lingo. Probably both. *shrugs*<br /><br /><b>Plot that I did not find to be a plot</b><br /><br />Was this book meant to be dark? If it was, it failed. A sexual awakening for the heroine, mixed in with some BDSM and kinky sex does <u>not</u> equate dark romance. You want dark? Go read Topping From Below or Her Master's Courtesan. For me, the book was hyped up to be a "dark read," which was the reason why I read it in the first place and when it ended up being more of a smutty guilty pleasure book, that feeling of disappointment is just....<i>disappointing.</i><br /><br />The main problem I had with this book though is this: <b>nearly 50% of the story is made up of filler sex.</b> I’m normally not critical of the amount of sex in a book because as long as it’s hot and steamy, it’s a plus for me. But for this book? No. With an amazing blurb like this story has and with key terms like “falling in love with stalker,” I expect to see plot development throughout the story on that aspect. <br /><br /><i>Why</i> does she fall in love with Twitch? (No, the answer is not because he’s fucking hot). <br /><i>Why</i> does he even stalk Lexi? <br /><i>Why</i> is he so intent on “breaking” Lexi? <br /><br />So many questions that needed to be answered, and quite frankly, there was no build up or plot development to get to that point. It was “bang, bang, filler sex, get to a point where Twitch says he needs to ‘tell the truth’ and BANG, truth, and then some.” So you have numerous detailed kinky sex scenes but everything else happened too suddenly without a good plot pace in between events. <br /><br /><b>The second huge problem I had with this book was Twitch himself.</b> I will concede that he’s messed up, maybe even twisted, but I feel like he tried too hard to be an evil devil rather it being in his nature. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The moment Lexi says she loves him, he turns into a love drunk boyfriend...for starters I didn’t even how he fell in love with her in the first place so there’s that. But really? For the first part of the book, he’s so intent on conquering her, branding her, and he makes a sudden 180 into an attentive boyfriend? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>This part I'm adding in after 24 hours of thinking about the events in the book, and also played a huge role in why I rated this book so lowly.</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[It's obvious to the reader after a good 10% that Twitch is Antonio Falco, the little boy from the prologue. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> As the reader, when I know this way ahead of time <i>before</i> Lexi knows it, it just makes her character more of a tool. Besides, the author dropped SO MANY hints throughout the book so it was incredulous that Lexi didn't connect the dots!!! ----&gt; Falco, <i>
  <b>Falcon</b>
</i> Industries? That bandage scene where they repeat the <i>exact</i> same words from the prologue? It may be a 20 year gap, BUT since Lexi said she thought of Antonio a lot through the years and that one scene in the prologue was their ONE time of communicating, how is it that she doesn't connect the dots? Way too many similarities and a TSTL naive female lead. <br /><br /><b>Another thing was Twitch’s <i>reasoning</i> behind the stalking.</b> This and the filler sex part is what made it a 2 star book for me. **WARNING** The spoiler tells you his reasoning so open at your own risk. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[In the prologue, a 6 year old Lexi helps an 8 year old Twitch by bandaging his wounds. This gave him “hope” for a better life, and just gave him hope in general. Later when he couldn’t find Lexi (because she moved) he became dejected and desperate, thus blaming LEXI for giving him hope. That sparks his agenda for tracking her down and worming himself into her life. He does that by hiring a dude to attack Lexi so he can come to her rescue. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />You know, I didn’t even mind the last part of the spoiler, after all, it makes this book kinda twisted and that’s cool as long as it was executed properly. But the reasoning? Seriously? Way too flimsy and I expected something <b>a LOT darker,</b> especially since the author dangled this part to the reader for a good 65% of the book. <br /><br /><b>Last thing: the ending.</b> *rubs head* I don’t mind that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[it’s not an HEA. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I expected it because the author did warn everyone in the blurb that this is a love story gone wrong. But hello? The last few lines of the book I need some serious clarification on. Is this supposed to be a standalone? Also it seemed like EVERYONE cried. Sorry I didn’t! When you smack me with that kind of ending and epilogue don’t expect me too. I think I was still in the dismal shock phase and never got out of it to cry. <br /><br /><u>So why not 1 star then?</u><br /><br />Because there WERE parts I genuinely liked. There are some fantastic quotes in here that you’ll probably see floating around on teasers and such so I think the author is a talented writer, just not the type of talented writer I can identify with.<br /><br /><b>The last thing I wanted to say is, there have been several concerns with a particular reader not liking this rating and proceeding to tell me how to rate it. Originally I had posted a portion of what this person said to me, but I took it down because I didn't want to confuse others into thinking I was addressing the author. I have several screenshots of the PM this person sent me, and if I were truly vindictive, I would've posted it for the entire GR community to see (comes with this person's name, full PM, etc) but I didn't because who wants a GR shitstorm when this is a place for readers alike to gather around and chat books?</b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15183359282164642176" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_816913132" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/816913132" />
    <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake"><img alt="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605987751p2/11626803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/816913132?book_show_action=true">Jan 08, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake">Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️</a>
      </span>

          marked it as dnf


          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940148861119" href="/book/show/18468559-raw">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer816913132" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6462685913365877404"><b>DNF @ 15%<br/><br/>Okay, sooooooo...<br/><br/>...this is awkward.</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455867903ra/18160134.gif' width='500' height='241' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>But I'm gonna go ahead and just call this one here. <br/><br/>Because otherwise, I would be ripping this thing to shreds. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455867903ra/18160135.gif' width='500' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And as highly entertaining as that has the potential to be...the <i>only reason</i> I would be finishing this would be so I could rate it and rip it to shreds. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455867903ra/18160136.gif' width='450' height='253' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Which would make me an asshole. <br/><br/>And mean. Verra mean. <br/><br/>And while I <i>am</i> aware that my profile name contains the word "bitchy," because TRUTH, there is a huge difference between being bitchy an</span>
  <span id="freeText6462685913365877404" style="display:none"><b>DNF @ 15%<br><br>Okay, sooooooo...<br><br>...this is awkward.</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455867903ra/18160134.gif" width="500" height="241" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But I'm gonna go ahead and just call this one here. <br><br>Because otherwise, I would be ripping this thing to shreds. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455867903ra/18160135.gif" width="500" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And as highly entertaining as that has the potential to be...the <i>only reason</i> I would be finishing this would be so I could rate it and rip it to shreds. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455867903ra/18160136.gif" width="450" height="253" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Which would make me an asshole. <br><br>And mean. Verra mean. <br><br>And while I <i>am</i> aware that my profile name contains the word "bitchy," because TRUTH, there is a huge difference between being bitchy and just plain cruel. <br><br>And besides, my "make people cry" quota is already full for the week, so...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455867903ra/18160137.gif" width="416" height="209" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>J fucking K people. <br><br>Anyway, this book. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455868848ra/18160186.gif" width="400" height="276" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was supposed to be "oooooooo" all dark and ish, but it was reading like a parody for me. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455868848ra/18160187.gif" width="295" height="216" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm that jackass in the back up there ^^^.<br><br>The writing style had a very tongue-in-cheek feel to it that just didn't jive with the tone I <i>felt</i> like the book was trying to go for. <br><br>And, speaking of the writing...I just didn't care for it, quite frankly. <br><br>Everything comes down to personal preference, as they say, and this just wasn't my cup of tea. <br><br>Or coffee...<br>Or wine...<br>Or vodka...<br>Or <s>rubbing alcohol</s> any ingestible form of liquid that I would actually drink. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455868848ra/18160188.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But the <i>main</i> reason I am calling it quits here?<br><br>Alexa.<br><br>Homegirl is a social worker, but what with how selflessly holier than thou she, as the narrator, portrays herself to be, you would think she majored in Super Woman and minored in Psychiatry. <br><br>When she first meets, Twitch *snort*, the H:<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"My type of work means I come across a lot of different types of people. I know that everyone is different, but what I'm sure about Twitch is that he's a sociopath."</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455870490ra/18160339.gif" width="425" height="239" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Really? Got that within five minutes did ya?<br><br>Impressive. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434930223ra/15279640.gif" width="500" height="223" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then...wait for this shit...regarding her neighbor:<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"George, my <b>bipolar</b> neighbor, would never lay a hand on me. The guy loves me! Being a [ermagherd!] <b>caseworker</b>, the first time we met, I picked up on his behavior right away. I'm sure he wasn't used to what he got from me.<br>A hug.<br>I told George that I worked with a lot of people who suffered mental illness, and that if he felt a panic attack coming on that I would be there for him..."</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455870490ra/18160340.gif" width="500" height="245" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I'm sorry. <br><br>It takes a lot to offend me. <br><br>But I grew up in a bipolar household. An immediate family member. <br>And it's not something that even highly trained psychiatrists can always notice "right away," let alone a simple social worker who thinks she's God's gift to humanity. <br><br>And to have the fucking audacity to trivialize something complex like that by presuming to say "I work with people with mental illness" - <i>like you, you poor thing!</i> - so come on over and have your panic attack (???) with me, your random fucking neighbor, whom you just met?!<br><br>Oh man, I'll be right fucking there, Super Woman! You hath cured me with your mere presence!<br><br>Thank FUCK you moved in!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1442571291ra/16253994.gif" width="320" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And THEN, when the friend DARES to suggest that poor bipolar George might be violent, listen to THIS response:<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"'Don't you do that, Nikki! That's not cool, babe."<br><br>'Do what?' she responds, exasperated.<br><br>Staring down a moment, I state, 'Stereotype.'"</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455870490ra/18160341.gif" width="400" height="216" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well, hey there, Pot. Why don't you go lecture Kettle some more about how not to be cookware. <br><br>Seriously, this was just fucking ridiculous and, like I said, I'm not going to be cruel and finish this thing knowing it's headed down a road I don't want to be on. <br><br>Because I'm not in the mood to hear about what dearest Alexa learned in Pysch 101. <br>And I'm not in the mood for self harm today either. <br><br>But anyway. Oh well! Win some/lose some!<br><br>MUAHH!<br><br>XXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXX<br><br><b>I was told that this book makes EVERYONE cry. <br>That it would make ME cry. <br><br>And to that person I say, did you not remember this about me?<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455176411i/18065685._SY540_.jpg" width="282" height="287.5" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I hardly EVER cry. <br>Even IRL. <br>But I swear I'm really soft inside my hard candy outer shell. *snort*<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455176411ra/18065686.gif" width="245" height="245" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440613939ra/15999714.gif" width="500" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Anycynic, when I hear the words "this will absolutely make you cry," my response is:<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455176411ra/18065687.gif" width="400" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Let's find out. </b></span>

<div id="review_734621702" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/734621702" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/734621702?book_show_action=true">Oct 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940148861119" href="/book/show/18468559-raw">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer734621702" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8943580821091397325"><b>5 RAW stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/4727de06-b4ff-4134-b8a6-0f66ae8bb393_zps7fc5eb33.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389088778i/7986811.jpg' alt='Raw photo 4727de06-b4ff-4134-b8a6-0f66ae8bb393_zps7fc5eb33.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>After reading Raw, thought to myself... ‘Is this really the same author that wrote The Friend-Zoned series?’ Wow! Talk about diverse writing styles! Although it did have a touch of humor, this book was much more dark than her previous works. And I loved it! I wouldn’t call it a dark and disturbing read, although it did have its moments... the words that come to mind when I think of this book are: intense, erotic, suspenseful, gritty and, well, RAW. It's not a happy love story. Bu</span>
  <span id="freeText8943580821091397325" style="display:none"><b>5 RAW stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/4727de06-b4ff-4134-b8a6-0f66ae8bb393_zps7fc5eb33.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389088778i/7986811.jpg" alt="Raw photo 4727de06-b4ff-4134-b8a6-0f66ae8bb393_zps7fc5eb33.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After reading Raw, thought to myself... ‘Is this really the same author that wrote The Friend-Zoned series?’ Wow! Talk about diverse writing styles! Although it did have a touch of humor, this book was much more dark than her previous works. And I loved it! I wouldn’t call it a dark and disturbing read, although it did have its moments... the words that come to mind when I think of this book are: intense, erotic, suspenseful, gritty and, well, RAW. It's not a happy love story. But hey, we we’re warned...<br><b>
  <blockquote>Author Note: This is not a love story. This is a story of a love gone wrong. </blockquote>
</b><br>Alexa is a good girl. She always has been. She had a rough life growing up, but it’s brought her to where she is today. A social worker helping other kids who don’t have it easy. She loves her job and her two best friends. Life is pretty good. Then she meets Twitch. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/6c8e320c-c16b-431d-a5b0-cf3b8568d105_zpse2b4dcc6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389088778i/7986812.jpg" alt="Raw photo 6c8e320c-c16b-431d-a5b0-cf3b8568d105_zpse2b4dcc6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Twitch has been watching (cough*stalking*cough) Alexa for a while now. She can feel him when he’s there. He wears a hood, but she knows it’s him. When she finally ‘meets’ Twitch, he saves her from someone attacking her. She should be afraid of him, maybe, but she’s not. <br><i>
  <blockquote>I know I should feel differently. I should feel uneasy. And even frightened. But I don’t know. Something about this man puts my mind at rest. And now I know deep down that I have nothing to fear. Twitch will protect me. Just like he always does.</blockquote>
</i><br>Twitch goes from being that anonymous watcher to someone who is present in Alexa’s life. He comes and goes as he pleases, but he is there with her. It’s comforting for her. She finds herself missing him when he’s not there. <br><br>Twitch is not a good guy. He knows that. He’s lived a rough life, and made his way from the bottom to the very top of the heap. He is successful, ruthless, and he looks the part- covered in tattoos. It was refreshing for me to have a ‘hero’ who wasn’t a hero at all. I love a villain. The anti-hero of the story. Those severely damaged and fucked up characters. Twitch fits the bill.<br><i>
  <blockquote>“You’re what fills the whole in my heart. You saved me. You’re my hero.”<br> “No. I’m not. You have no idea how wrong you are. What you want me to be... I can’t ever be. It’s not me. I’m the villain in this story.”</blockquote>
</i><br> Regardless, Lexi finds herself still wanting him. Things with Twitch are different than anything she’s used to, but he did give her fair warning.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/c4d8c8f4-62d8-450f-b45f-edf0727eaf11_zps8b8fc457.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389088778i/7986813.jpg" alt="Raw photo c4d8c8f4-62d8-450f-b45f-edf0727eaf11_zps8b8fc457.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Twitch and Lexi together... they were combustable. It was erotic, dirty, sexy, steamy and down right HOT. Rough uninhibited sex. It’s unlike anything Lexi has ever experienced. She is shocked with how much she likes it. The things that Twitch does to her, things that should scare her to death, they don't. Well, maybe they scare her a bit but mostly they turn her on. Twitch is more surprised than Lexi. This he was not expecting. Lexi is a contradiction to him. <br><br> <a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/ea16c4f2-175f-42df-a735-b4aaec15466b_zps40690d98.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389088778i/7986814.jpg" alt="Raw photo ea16c4f2-175f-42df-a735-b4aaec15466b_zps40690d98.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Lexi is ruined by Twitch, just as he wanted. She can’t think of anything or anyone else besides him. She knows she’ll never want to be with anyone besides him again. Full of secrets, Twitch doesn’t know how he feels. One minute he wants to ruin Lexi, the next he wants her forever. He has issues. But thats why I love him. Now to that ending. I will admit, I cried when reading it. I’m not one of those people who needs a sunshine and rainbows happy ever after every time I read a book. That’s just not how it goes all the time. Did I love how the book ended? No. But still, I’m OKAY with the ending. I am, however, hoping the author decides to write a second book. I think there is so much more of Twitch and Lexi’s story to tell! This book will have your heart beating out of your chest. There were a few things I found out that had me in a state of shock. The author is correct. This is a story of a love gone wrong...<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/9e97433a-ece1-4c2c-a9cb-f72f9842663f_zps537f8be4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389088778i/7986815.jpg" alt="Raw photo 9e97433a-ece1-4c2c-a9cb-f72f9842663f_zps537f8be4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I would highly recommended this book to anyone looking for an intense, unconventional, powerful and tantalizing read. If that sounds like your cup of tea- pick this up. If you’re looking for Aurora’s normal lighter, fluffy, sweet and comical stuff, this probably isn’t the book for you! It’s a well written, highly entertaining 5 star read! </span>
  <a data-text-id="8943580821091397325" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer768819096" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer9632192534399824776">OMG....that ending.....I'm blinking back tears and pissed off at the same time!! I don't see a #2 in Belle's shelves.....Gotta have a #2......Gotta digest this.<br/><br/>I can't write a review of this book...for the past hour I have sat staring at my Word Doc ---- typing....deleting....typing.....deleting. My review will not be able to do this book justice.<br/><br/>I can't put into words what I felt about this book - because it keeps coming out as a jumble of thoughts which make no sense.<br/><br/>I just want to make clear </span>
  <span id="freeText9632192534399824776" style="display:none">OMG....that ending.....I'm blinking back tears and pissed off at the same time!! I don't see a #2 in Belle's shelves.....Gotta have a #2......Gotta digest this.<br /><br />I can't write a review of this book...for the past hour I have sat staring at my Word Doc ---- typing....deleting....typing.....deleting. My review will not be able to do this book justice.<br /><br />I can't put into words what I felt about this book - because it keeps coming out as a jumble of thoughts which make no sense.<br /><br />I just want to make clear though...that up until 50% of this book, I felt like I was still in a book slump and couldn't connect.<br /><br />50% on.....I fell in love<br /><br />The end - Ummmmm...NO - I WANT MORE!!!<br /><br />If you see this Ms. Aurora...hear me now - if I do not see a sequel to this ---- I will find you ----- I will stalk you ----- I will be in your dreams ---- every time you open your eyes, you will see ME ----- and I will be haunting your every move with words whispered in your ear...."BOOK 2....BOOK 2.....MORE TWITCH.....BOOK 2"<br /><br />I WILL BE YOUR TWITCH!! ;-)<br /><br />Ciao'</span>
  <a data-text-id="9632192534399824776" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer719508543" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9174579194426579552">4 STARS out of 5<br/>(spoilers are hidden and close to end of review)<br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388763765ra/7923634.gif' alt=' photo SHOCKER1_zps284d25ee.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>Review</u>
</b><br/><br/><b>DAMN THAT ENDING TO ALLLLLL HELL. WHY? WHY? WHYYYYYYY?</b><br/><br/><i>‘Some things in life are so sad that there are no words to describe the amount of sadness, grief, and sorrow a person is feeling. I assume this is why God allowed humans the simple act of crying. When a person cries, they feel the sadness slowly ease out of them. They feel as though they are justifiably respecting a person that has died through showing their grief. They</i></span>
  <span id="freeText9174579194426579552" style="display:none">4 STARS out of 5<br>(spoilers are hidden and close to end of review)<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388763765ra/7923634.gif" alt=" photo SHOCKER1_zps284d25ee.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <u>Review</u>
</b><br><br><b>DAMN THAT ENDING TO ALLLLLL HELL. WHY? WHY? WHYYYYYYY?</b><br><br><i>‘Some things in life are so sad that there are no words to describe the amount of sadness, grief, and sorrow a person is feeling. I assume this is why God allowed humans the simple act of crying. When a person cries, they feel the sadness slowly ease out of them. They feel as though they are justifiably respecting a person that has died through showing their grief. They allow a moment of sorrow to overcome them and cry out a small portion of their unseen pain.’</i> -Alexa<br><br>First of all this book<b> DESTROYED ME</b> and words…words<b> FAILED ME</b> by the end. I don’t think I have ever been so flustered when writing a review as I am with this one there was things I liked and some things I did not like.(I’ll expand on that later) One thing’s for sure, I was warned by the author as are you. <br><b>***Author Note: This is not a love story. This is a story of love gone wrong.***</b> <br><br>Definitely safe to say I got what I asked for.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388720087i/7908628.jpg" alt=" photo RAWCOLLAGEfinal_zps0cce7e2c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i><b>“Monsters don’t always lurk in the shadows.”</b> Reaching up, he runs a fingertip slowly down the length of my jaw. Leaning forward, his breath warms me as he mutters a hairs-breadth away from my lips,<b> “Sometimes they hide in plain sight.”</b></i><br><br>Alexa Ballentine is an American working in Australia as a case/social worker. She considers her kids her cubs, she deeply cares for their well being and it shows in her actions. In fact I don’t think there is <b>one</b> bad bone in Alexa’s body. Coming from two parents who were not parents at all she personally knows from experience how bad it can be out on the streets. <br><br>Alexa is also aware of<b> him</b>; watching her. He’s been doing it for some time now and she can feel his eyes on her whenever he is near.<br> <br><b>He</b> is the eyes under the hoodie.<br><br><i>I need her. I want her. I will own her.’</i> -Twitch<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388766494i/7924437.jpg" alt=" photo twitchTeaseNovHoodpic_zps6e526e41.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is where things get complicated. Something bad happens and it brings hoodie stalker guy up close and personal with Alexa. <br><br><i>‘That’s when he does something I’ve been wishing for <b>forever</b>. <br>He lowers the hood.’</i><br><br>And dude is FRIGHTENING. Scares her, scares me, it gets real. You have no idea what will happen.<br><br><i>‘Opening my eyes to find his still on my face, I ask a hushed,<b> “What’s your name?”</b> The corner of his lip tips up.<b> “Doesn’t matter. You’ll forget it once I’m gone.”</b> Taking a small step towards him, I promise,<b> “No, I won’t.”</b> It’s his turn to take a step back. He watches me some more. Those eyes. It feels as if they see everything. Breathing in, he replies on an exhale, <b>“I’m Twitch.”</b></i><br><br>We meet the guy in the hood. His name is Twitch and he has an itch so to speak for Alexa. <br><br>She wants him. <br><br><i>There’s something animalistic about this man. Something I want to be a part of. Something I want to be included in. He’s a force of nature.’</i> -Alexa<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388766494ra/7924438.gif" alt=" photo ORGASMICGIF1_zpse64871e1-1.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The attraction is very clear and she lets him know. Twitch is very up front with Alexa when he tells her what he is about and uhhh how he likes it. DIRTY.<br><br>As readers take in both pov’s we learn that Twitch has an agenda. He wants to break Alexa, but why?<br><br><i>‘There’s something about having your choices taken from you that is equally liberating and frightening. Handing over control to a person is a big deal. A showing of trust. And sometimes, I would like to be taken on a ride rather than drive.’</i> -Alexa<br><br><b>
  <u>My Sweet and Sour</u>
</b><br><br><b>My Sweet</b> - I enjoyed how Belle Aurora gave us snippets of personality with the internal monologues. I found it witty and entertaining.<br><br><b>My Sour</b> - Well my first choice is too spoilerish so here is my second choice, mean Twitch… I did not like mean Twitch at all.<br><br>This is the first time secondary characters made the book for me and the main characters just seemed to give me a splitting headache. I was so unsure on how to rate RAW. Why? Well for one, I struggled with the hero, Twitch and his motives towards Alexa. More so the reasoning behind it. Second, Alexa and her internal battle with allowing Twitch to Dominate her.. It seemed like she fought it throughout the entire book and I just did not get that about her. <br><br>Either your down or not. Her actions spoke volumes though..She was DEFINITELY down. So why internally fight it, just accept it. Maybe that is easier said then done, don't know.<br><br><u>My Thoughts</u><br>Basically I was unhappy with the reasoning Twitch used for going after Alexa. Yes, I understand his anger but I feel as if he chose Alexa without just cause. His anger was completely misdirected. So maybe it was just me. I don’t know, it just felt wrong… Some may argue that <b>that</b> is the point, it was misdirected, that’s the tragedy of it all. And I guess *shrugs a shoulder* I can see how people feel that way.<br><br>I sort of thought there was a few plot holes. <br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>- How was Twitch able to just set up shop like that in a whole new country with a cover company and so on and so forth? Drug empire’s are not built over night. <br><br>- Why did Twitch wait so long to enter Alexa’s life. He said it took a year to find her, ok so how soon was he in Australia after that?<br> <br>- If he was watching her for so long how did he fail pick up on the fact that she is such a sweet, good hearted person. Was he blinded by his rage? Possible. Why not explore that a bit more? Or is all this a result of his brain injury?<br><br>-Why did she not further question Ling living with him? That irked me the way she dropped it.<br><br>-His stealth missions in and out of her house? How? Guess that falls in to his mysterious ways category huh?<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>My Rating and Why</b><br>4 STARS- I wanted more. I felt these things could have been explored upon maybe cut out a few sex scenes. OH MY, I can’t believe I just said that… I NEVER opt to cut out sex. However, it would have upped my rating if I had these answers of this I am sure.<br><br><u>My Ratings</u><br><b>Characters-</b> Likeable<br><b>Writing Style-</b> Good<br><b>Plot/Storyline-</b> Guy wants to break girl, girl wants to be controlled. Can these two find love? Real love?<br><b>Steam Factor-</b> High/Very Steamy on a scale of 1-10 I say 9<br><b>Overall-</b> I liked it!<br><b>My Recommendation:</b> READ AT YOUR OWN RISK!<br><b><br>Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br><b>For more reviews got to:</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">www.realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot...</a> <br><br><br><b>**ARC provided by author in exchange for an honest review**</b><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/815497200?book_show_action=true">Jan 07, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sammy Loves Books" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sammy Loves Books" href="/user/show/14227114-sammy-loves-books">Sammy Loves Books</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Sammy by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/11075747-nikki-navareus">Nikki ღ Navareus</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer815497200" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15345638397948602827">*****Spoiler Alert*****Spoiler Alert******Spoiler Alert*****<br/><b>
  <blockquote>"Monsters don't always lurk in the shadows"…"Sometimes they hide in plain sight"</blockquote>
</b><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390053443i/8135465._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='600' alt='twitch' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Lexi has a stalker named Twitch. And she kinda likes it. One night she is viciously attacked outside her apartment, and her stalker becomes her savior. Then her savior becomes her lover.<br/><b>
  <blockquote>God. This guy has me so hot and bothered I actually feel tipsy.</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/>I was all wrapped up in the story until learning Twitch was a brooding millionaire. That liked rough s</span>
  <span id="freeText15345638397948602827" style="display:none">*****Spoiler Alert*****Spoiler Alert******Spoiler Alert*****<br><b>
  <blockquote>"Monsters don't always lurk in the shadows"…"Sometimes they hide in plain sight"</blockquote>
</b><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390053443i/8135465._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="600" alt="twitch" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lexi has a stalker named Twitch. And she kinda likes it. One night she is viciously attacked outside her apartment, and her stalker becomes her savior. Then her savior becomes her lover.<br><b>
  <blockquote>God. This guy has me so hot and bothered I actually feel tipsy.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>I was all wrapped up in the story until learning Twitch was a brooding millionaire. That liked rough sex. I rolled my eyes and thought, "Oh no, another fifty shades rip off". But not quite.. Twitch is a true sociopath. Breaking the law, torture, and murder are acceptable ends to a mean. His obsession with breaking Alexa becomes his downfall.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390053443i/8135466._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="600" alt="suit" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"You don't get to kiss me until I say you can" </blockquote>
</b><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389886648ra/8081788.gif" width="400" height="224" alt="smiling" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"You feeling uncomfortable?"…"Good. Get used to it. Because I'm going to do bad things to you." </blockquote>
</b><br><br><br>Twitch soon discovers Lexi isn't the villain that he has created in his mind. She was just an innocent six year old girl that helped bandage him up after his father abused him. Lexi is an angel at heart. She doesn't judge others and she puts others needs before her own. Twitches goal has been to hurt her and cause her pain. Which is pretty fucked up in my opinion.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436552i/882352.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="lexi" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mostly due to foreshadowing, there were a few plot twists through out the book that I felt were predictable. Some were entertaining, but predictable. I also knew deep in my gut that this could only end tragically. And it did. <br><br><b>Mega Eye Roll /Unrealistic Moments <br><br>There were too many eye roll moments for me while reading this book. I will place these under a spoiler tag, even though this review is already hidden. I don't suggest you read these spoilers that irked me unless you have read the book. Because this will definitely ruin it for you.</b><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>1, the whole "I'm a drug dealing king pin" that kills snitches… and cuts eyeballs out with a switchblade would have been fine, but they had to go and make Twitch a millionaire.<br><br>2, the whole "I'm a millionaire thing" who lives in a mansion and throws masquerade parties, (I'm so tired of that angle) because otherwise women wouldn't put up with crazy ass motherfuckers that like to "fuck dirty" and mess with their minds, unless they are rich. Then everything they do is forgiven. (because they are hot and rich)<br><br>3, I knew that Twitch had hired Lexi's attacker to sexually assault Lexi long before the truth came out. It was so obvious. That was his way in from stalker, to savior. The fact that he did that disgusts me and was almost a deal breaker. Even though he wanted to hurt Lexi, his obsession with her made no sense. It also DISGUSTS me that any hero would ever plot to hurt/harm/abuse the heroine.<br><br><b>And this should have been #1..Twitches reason for wanting to hurt Lexi was a joke. He wanted to hurt her because she was nice to him once when he was eight years old, and gave him hope of a better life? So he wanted to "break" her. Because how dare she give him hope!! WTF? That's a horribly weak plot!</b><br><br>4, Oh and the moment Twitch cut that man's eyeball out and left him alive…..I knew the book would end tragically!! There is a thing called revenge!!! A real Sociopath would know this.<br><br>5, So Lexi takes her birth control pills daily, until she starts to have UNPROTECTED SEX on a Daily basis with a man she doesn't know, and then she forgets to take her pills……and gets pregnant…riiiiight… Big Ass Eye Roll Moment<br><br><b><blockquote>“You’ve been fucking me for months and you don’t even know my name. Who does that?</blockquote></b><br>That's a Damn Good question!!!<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390053443i/8135467._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="600" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>6, So you hire a kid to get him off the streets from dealing, only to send him on a drug run with Happy. I knew Michael was gonna end up dead when he started working for Twitch.<br><br>7. Final eye roll…how do you fake a death while in a coma, cause I know that Lexi probably never left his side. So did he wake up the one moment she did leave the hospital and tell Happy, "Hey, lets fake my death to keep her and the baby safe" And there was no reason to fake his death after the One Eyed man was dead? Right? <br><br><b>The Epilogue</b><br><br>Twitch as a sociopath was pretty spot on, until the end when Twitch states that he "cried like a baby" when he saw his son with markers on his hand. That shit was touching as hell. I got misty too. But that is not true to the character of a sociopath.<br><br>A true sociopath would not deny himself being with Lexi and his son. They are too selfish to do that. Twitch tried to push Lexi away in his office by telling her that he had hired that man to rape her, only to change his mind (3 minutes later) before she got to the elevator. Sociopaths are not saints that are able to put the needs of others first. There is no way Twitch could have stated away for 5 years. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>There was no Happy Ever After!!! <br>Maybe there will be a book #2, maybe not.<br><br>This would have been a solid 4 star if I hadn't rolled my eyes so much at how "over the top" Twitch was. And the lack of a HEA is ALWAYS a deal breaker for me unless I know it's going to be a trilogy.<br><br>I Must say that this writer's flow was very smooth. I never had to re-read passages, or stumble over anything. Her thoughts were clear and precise. And I loved the switch in POV's. My 2 star review is NO reflection of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6983012.Belle_Aurora" title="Belle Aurora" rel="nofollow noopener">Belle Aurora</a>'s writing style. Just the plot. I would definitely consider reading another of her books!!!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

I really enjoyed this reading Raw, Twitch and Lexi were hilarious and infuriating at times, but I had to know their story and where it would go!<br><br>She's a social worker who has a soft spot for kids who've been forced onto the streets because of life at home. This makes sense since her childhood was almost exactly the same. He's a successful "businessman". While out one day she's attacked and Twitch comes to her rescue, this is the beginning of a compelling relationship, Twitch is intense and broody both in public and in the bedroom, he's all alpha male.<br><br>He's also a crazy, hot, domineering, panty-melting, ovary-busting asshole; and I really liked him!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389112350ra/7990669.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lexi is sweet, quirky and can be a dork at times, she's the ying to he's yang.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389112350ra/7990670.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Once he allowed her to see him, she really didn't have a chance. She was literally putty in his hands, and any inconsistencies with his story were over looked. She was mesmerised.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389112350ra/7990671.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I laughed, I got angry, I wanted to slap some sense into them and I thoroughly enjoyed it! This book is engaging, it had a touch of humour that I found refreshing (this is huge, because I don't like humour)I enjoyed the writing immensely and will definitely be reading more of this author's work.<br><br>P.S. I hope there's a book 2 (because that's the more I want to read)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389112350ra/7990672.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16644411147076978911"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386956402i/7492287._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Title:</b> Raw<br/><b>Series:</b> Standalone<br/><b>Author:</b> Belle Aurora<br/><b>Release Date: </b> January 3rd, 2014<br/><b>Rating:</b> 4.5 stars<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ No  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386956402i/7492288._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Sweet, heartwarming and hilarious Belle Aurora is officially gone and I’m not sure if I mourned her for a single second. As much as I adored her previous novels, this time she not only astounded me but also showed me how talented she truly is. In Raw she not only challenged herself, completely changing her usual style of writing from easygoing,</span>
  <span id="freeText16644411147076978911" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386956402i/7492287._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title:</b> Raw<br><b>Series:</b> Standalone<br><b>Author:</b> Belle Aurora<br><b>Release Date: </b> January 3rd, 2014<br><b>Rating:</b> 4.5 stars<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ No  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386956402i/7492288._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sweet, heartwarming and hilarious Belle Aurora is officially gone and I’m not sure if I mourned her for a single second. As much as I adored her previous novels, this time she not only astounded me but also showed me how talented she truly is. In Raw she not only challenged herself, completely changing her usual style of writing from easygoing, snarky prose to something fifty shades of darker, she also challenged her readers, and I’m glad I took this test! Belle Aurora didn’t have a single struggle with writing in entirely different genre. My respect for her only grew. <br><br>Raw was gritty read. Fabulously wild story that took me on the verge of sanity and made me step out of my comfort zone more than once. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388783288i/7928951.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was overwhelmed. Stunned. Dazed. Dared. I felt unimaginable pain, fear, shock and discomfort. I was thrown on wild, rough, never ending, the most fucked up ride of my life. Ride that made me forget about everything only to make me feel. Feel so many deliciously dark and forbidden emotions, emotions that were bleeding from Belle Aurora’s novel. And I loved every minute of it. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “You’re nobody ‘til somebody loves you.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>This story follows Alexa. She’s sweet, good person. She’s happy. She has loveable friends, great work and nice apartment. She also has a stalker. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388783288i/7928952.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Twitch is a guy that picture would pop up if you google ‘bad boy’ ‘antihero’ ‘villain’ or ‘stay away from’. He’s damaged. He’s broken. He’s certainly not a good human being. Yet Lexi is drawn to him and quickly finds herself falling for a man that doesn’t deserve her.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “Not everyone can be a fairy-tale hero.” He pauses a moment, then adds, “The world needs villains too.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388783288i/7928953.png" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am pleased, that I finally found a book with a man that is not only so called bad boy wannabe. He is bad and period. No questions asked. <br><br>This is a great addition to the story, because it makes it realistic. Belle Aurora made a great job in creating characters. Their entirely opposite personalities were well thought and brilliant!<br><br>Raw is not a fluffy love story. Raw is not your usual romance. Raw isn’t a novel you can easily label or name. There isn’t a single page that doesn’t dare readers and make them think. <br><br>In single, yet so meaningful plot, Aurora catches the truth of life and she doesn’t need a ‘knight in shining armor’ hero to picture true love. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388783288i/7928954.png" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>While being sexy, controversial and so, so hot, Raw was everything I could ask for. I am immensely glad I picked it up and opened myslef for this wonderful erotic experience. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Monsters don't always lurk in the shadows. Sometimes they hide in plain sight.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386956727i/7492465._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388710486i/7906635._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo unnamed_zps167d69f1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I feel like someone came and kicked me in my chest as hard as they could and leaving me there to care for myself. Honestly that is how I feel right now. It is so hard to come to terms with what I just read and type it down. <br><br>All I know is that this is my first 5 star book I have read in 2014. I couldn't have asked for more of a perfect book, I couldn't. There is nothing I would have changed. Maybe something but when I think about it I am sad and happy at the same time. I know.... That is one thing I do know is that. Doesn't make any sense of me saying that when you have no idea what I am talking about but once you read it you will get me. <br><br>It has been a long time since I have read a couple that compares to Twitch and Lexi. I think it has been years. Maybe never really. It just takes me that deep that I just can't compare it to any other book or character. Both of these two characters are fucked up in their own way. I feel like their relationship is so unique that is is hard not to love it and want everything to come out happy roses and everyone dances. It's fucking <b> RAW </b>. The title speaks for it self. It comes down to that it is fucking damn raw and I love it that much more. I love when I start reading a book and I can't put it down for the life of me. I have to finish it just to know what is going to happen. I felt this sick feeling in my stomach through the whole thing cause it is not like any book I have read. You have no idea what is going to happen. It takes you by surprise and leaves you feeling like I said someone kicked you in the fucking chest. I do not regret anything on this. Just that I wish I would have took my time instead of being greedy and devouring the fucking book in one night. <br><br><blockquote> <b> “Monsters don't always lurk in the shadows. Sometimes they hide in plain sight.” </b>
</blockquote>  <br><br>I am not quite sure where it came from that this book is dark. I know everyone has their own titles on what they think is dark. To me this is not dark in no way shape or form. I never got that feel from this book and nothing made me think that it was dark. I love my dark reads those are my favorite. I am glad that I was not told this book was dark before I read it because then I would have gotten a more hyped up of the darkness that was suppose to be coming out of it. So I am glad that I did not hear that before I read it. But it kind of throws me off that some say this is dark. Anyhow just wanted to throw that out there..... <br><br>Twitch, is not the good guy in this book. He is the villain and I must say I fucking love the villains the most. For some reason they draw my attention more then the good ones. And fuck man, Twitch makes the perfect fucking villain. I could keep him and eat him up all day long. Yes he is that perfect to me. He does fucked up shit and it seems kind of crazy but hey I love it. Don't judge me. :) <br><br><a href="http://s1287.photobucket.com/user/bauswella/media/PicMonkeyCollage_zpsed2a63cd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388710486i/7906636._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo PicMonkeyCollage_zpsed2a63cd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I swear within the first couple of pages of this book I my heart was already in it. It is very heart wrenching when reading it at time. Kind of chokes me up still just thinking about this book. <br><br>I couldn't have asked for a better book to start my year. The author did an amazing job creating such a beautiful fucked up story. Even in authors note got me thinking this will take me on a ride. <b> ***Author Note: This is not a love story. This is a story of love gone wrong.*** </b> Right there I fucking knew this book would not be leaving me anytime soon and it will stick with me for a long time. It's one of those books that I can't re-read over and over but it is something that I know I have loved and will read it again just because it had kept with me. <br><br><i> ARC provided by author exchanged for honest review. </i><br><br><a href="http://www.thereadingroomblog.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1461870048i/18922777.png" alt=" photo Follow the Readng Rom Blog_zpsznrkrqks.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/thereadingroombookblog/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1461870152i/18922804.png" alt=" photo Like the Reading ROom Blog on Fb_zpsnigjcua7.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17248424918019046429" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
