<div id="review_812481547" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/812481547" />
    <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr"><img alt="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465384674p2/9080319.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/812481547?book_show_action=true">Jan 04, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940148861119" href="/book/show/18468559-raw">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr?shelf=best-of-2014">best-of-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer812481547" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16286169082011194518">Fan-freaking-tastic! I was shaking at that ending! After calming myself for 12 hours to decompress, here we go...<br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20from%20AE/tumblr_mepwx8xCUn1rybq9m_zps00582171.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389151459ra/7995608.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_mepwx8xCUn1rybq9m_zps00582171.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&current=1f3698226d064b670533c433981fdf55_zps4e767736.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389191346i/8002714._SY540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Do you like a book that's a little dirty? Ya know, where it's not all hearts and flowers, the sex isn't missionary with soothing music by Sinatra? Where the hero is really an anti-hero who starts out on a mission of revenge and ends up falling for his victim? Yes? Well, then Raw is the book for you!<br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&current=6701f26ddced6abaf666f8e650b94845_zps29724b58.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389192067i/8002822._SY540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>After reading Willing Captive by Belle Aurora, I knew I had to read this. H</span>
  <span id="freeText16286169082011194518" style="display:none">Fan-freaking-tastic! I was shaking at that ending! After calming myself for 12 hours to decompress, here we go...<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20from%20AE/tumblr_mepwx8xCUn1rybq9m_zps00582171.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389151459ra/7995608.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mepwx8xCUn1rybq9m_zps00582171.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=1f3698226d064b670533c433981fdf55_zps4e767736.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389191346i/8002714._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Do you like a book that's a little dirty? Ya know, where it's not all hearts and flowers, the sex isn't missionary with soothing music by Sinatra? Where the hero is really an anti-hero who starts out on a mission of revenge and ends up falling for his victim? Yes? Well, then Raw is the book for you!<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=6701f26ddced6abaf666f8e650b94845_zps29724b58.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389192067i/8002822._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After reading Willing Captive by Belle Aurora, I knew I had to read this. Her writing style is raw and gritty for sure. It captives the reader immediately, leaving you incapable of putting the book down. <br><br>So many reviews posted Ms. Aurora's warning at the start of this book- <br><br><b>"This is not a love story. This is a story of love gone bad."</b><br><br>I don't agree entirely. I think this sets the reader up that love won't occur in this book. It does, so that, in my humble opinion, makes this a love story. A torturous love story. That quote I worry sets it up so people won't take the chance on it. <br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=1b412bee1ed264f9d2efaa050df55148_zps5e0269f8.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389192067i/8002823._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I'd rather quote her dedication of this book because it sums it up perfectly to me.<br><br><b>"To anyone who has ever loved unconditionally. To all the people who have loved someone who did not deserve it. And finally, to every person who has followed their heart down the path less travelled. This is for you."</b><br><br>I devoured this book. When I dove in, I didn't come up for air. It's mysterious and captivating right up to the end. There are still a couple questions not answered in my head though. I'd honestly avoid reading a ton of reviews for this as EVERYONE barks at the lack of a HEA. Well, the ending will leave you shaking, that's for sure. But not official negative closure and the last three sentences of the book leave me with hope for a future book...<br><br>The feelings I was left with deep inside after reading Raw was mostly rawness. Funny she chose that as the title because it's perfect. Lexi is a social worker who notices this hooded man watching her day after day. He never makes a move, in fact, she almost gets a sense of safety from his gaze. When one day this hooded enigma saves her from a sexual assault, she's even more drawn to his protective persona. Not to mention, when the hood comes down, he's gorgeous- all tattooed, clean smelling, muscular...hot. And his name is Trink....<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=abb8ff867dd5b3cec0b45b463cbc3176_zps0f502a72.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389192067i/8002824._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>That's all you're getting. Read it. Unless you're a total hearts and flowers romance reader, I do NOT think the ending is that bad. I also wouldn't call this book that dark AT ALL. I look forward to reading Willing Captive after reading this gem!<br><br>A book that evokes the feelings this one did in me deserves to be hailed! I applaud Belle Aurora. On a comparative sense, I do not think this book's ending was non-HEA like Blind Obsession by Ella Frank. Everyone talked of that non-HEA. This one leaves me with hope...just read the last three sentences! In the mean time, I'll pick up my heart off the floor and trudge on. Until we see you again Twitch and Lexi...because I WILL see you again...</span>
  <a data-text-id="16286169082011194518" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer13250313739016954511"><b>DNF at 50% ..</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390261888ra/8178871.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I don't know if I got the April Fools addition or just a bad case of PMSing but this book was <b> NOT</b> an entertaining read for me. I was excited to start RAW after seeing rave review after rave review on my feed for weeks . In fact, this nosey bitch did not open a single spoiler because I couldn't wait to cry and have an emotional breakdown of my very own....yeah, I'm weird like that. Unfortunately the only thing I felt was ABSOLUTE annoyance thanks to <b>Lexi's</b> absurd behavior, and you c</span>
  <span id="freeText13250313739016954511" style="display:none"><b>DNF at 50% ..</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390261888ra/8178871.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't know if I got the April Fools addition or just a bad case of PMSing but this book was <b> NOT</b> an entertaining read for me. I was excited to start RAW after seeing rave review after rave review on my feed for weeks . In fact, this nosey bitch did not open a single spoiler because I couldn't wait to cry and have an emotional breakdown of my very own....yeah, I'm weird like that. Unfortunately the only thing I felt was ABSOLUTE annoyance thanks to <b>Lexi's</b> absurd behavior, and you can think I'm being harsh all you like, as even the character called herself pitiful, stupid and pathetic. I found everything about her to be <br> <b> I-R-R-I-T-A-T-I-N-G! </b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390261801ra/8178847.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now onto <b>Twitch</b> I felt nothing for his character. I love me some tats, and his piercing were a definite plus but my vaj requires more than that . I didn't get a single ladyboner while reading. I'm fairly certain that had more to do with Lexi being present than lack of character appeal. Yes, he was cruel, arrogant, mischievous brute but I never disliked him. How could I get upset at Twitch when Lexi so desperately wanted him? Exactly, I couldn't. I kept waiting for Twitch to say "Come on,it's time to see the wizard. "...........<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390349827ra/8195802.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> ...<b> NO KIDDING! </b> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384726459ra/6941415.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, once the only thing twitching was my pulsating headache and I had lost all- my- fuck- to -give regarding his vendetta, I knew it was time to say "I'm done". So I did. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390262825ra/8179042.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> PLEASE </b> don't let my opinions deter you from reading RAW. I have very, VERY little patience for naïve heroines. The reviews are amazing. Apparently I just wasn't in the mood for this type of story ..<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390264596ra/8179242.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>

<div id="review_736018833" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/736018833" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/736018833?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>

<div id="review_716395742" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/716395742" />
    <a title="Zakirrah BookBlogger" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15894726-zakirrah-bookblogger"><img alt="Zakirrah BookBlogger" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396291066p2/15894726.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/716395742?book_show_action=true">Sep 10, 2013</a>

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940148861119" href="/book/show/18468559-raw">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15894726-zakirrah-bookblogger?shelf=arc-or-netgalley">arc-or-netgalley</a>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer716395742" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8680273454789016834"><b>5 TWISTED, DAMAGED, ADDICTIVE STARS!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388769941i/7925610.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>This is how it began..<br/><br/><b>JUST DROPPED EVERYTHING..hellooo book *strokes phone* I have been waiting a long time for you (weird evil accent is being used) *kissy faces* </b><br/><br/>This is how it ended..<br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403256ra/784470.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>YOU BROKE ME BELLE!</b> I kind of hate you right now but I still love ya!<br/>when I saw <b>***Author Note: This is not a love story. This is a story of love gone wrong.***</b> my brain was like hah! its lies don't believe it, things always work out in Belle's books.right? RIGHT? ..oh hell n</span>
  <span id="freeText8680273454789016834" style="display:none"><b>5 TWISTED, DAMAGED, ADDICTIVE STARS!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388769941i/7925610.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This is how it began..<br><br><b>JUST DROPPED EVERYTHING..hellooo book *strokes phone* I have been waiting a long time for you (weird evil accent is being used) *kissy faces* </b><br><br>This is how it ended..<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403256ra/784470.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>YOU BROKE ME BELLE!</b> I kind of hate you right now but I still love ya!<br>when I saw <b>***Author Note: This is not a love story. This is a story of love gone wrong.***</b> my brain was like hah! its lies don't believe it, things always work out in Belle's books.right? RIGHT? ..oh hell no coz I was sooo wrong! Stupid little voice in my head trying to get me killed but I'm so glad I read this book because omg it's brilliant!<br><br>I usually stick to my happily ever afters, like come on don't we have enough bad shit in real life, why read about sad things huh? But then I have them days where I pick up a book and say break my heart baby..okay I don't really..I don't talk to books..pfft nah that ain't me.. <br>But yeah sometimes you read a book that breaks your heart, turns you into an emotional mess and leaves you thinking about it for <s>Months and years</s> days later and having the whole story flash in your mind and it haunts you all over again.<br><br><b>You’re nobody ‘til somebody loves you.</b><br><br>This isn't your normal love story, it won't leave you with bubbles of happiness and rainbows..nah it will crush you, haunt you, stalk you ;)<br>Right from the start the story gripped me and it never let me go.I finished this book all in one day as I couldn't stop reading it, even though at times I was confused, hurt angry and so many other emotions that I can't even name. <br><br><b>Addiction:-</b><br>The condition of being habitually or compulsively occupied with or or involved in something.<br><b>Synonyms:</b>	dependency, dependence, craving, habit, weakness, compulsion, fixation, enslavement<br><br>This is a story of an addict, of abuse, of hope, of destruction.<br>This is a story of two people being link by hurt, two people desperate to fill the void in their lives.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388773618i/7926591.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>“We’re all addicted to something that takes away the pain.” </b><br><br>The characters are damaged both Lexi and Twitch have had a tough life.Their relationship is dysfunctional, colossal mess of hurt, love,lust, anger and yet there is so much more to it. Twitch..Oh Twitch my heart ached for him, for what he went through. I wanted to reach into the book and give him a big hug and make him feel loved because that's what he needed, what he lived without for too long. But then there were times I wanted to punch him in the face and scream at him for not being open, for not communicating, for being so damn hard to read!!<br><br><b>“Monsters don't always lurk in the shadows. Sometimes they hide in plain sight.” </b><br><br>Lexi was a strong character, I really liked her even though I sometimes felt like omg why would you let him do that? Twitch became her weakness and in a way he was as much of her addiction as she was his.Being a victim of abuse, that will always stay with you no matter how old you get, no matter what happens. You can either live life thinking about it daily and being bitter about it or you can make something of yourself.You can rise above it.You can change and give someone the hope and help you never got. Lexi fell into the right side where as Twitch fell into the bad..but who are we to put people into boxes? Life is full of choices and this story shows you how your choices bring consequences sometimes good and sometimes bad.<br><br>Twitch isn't a hero.Twitch needs help. He won't save you if he is here to punish you.<br>First book of 2014 and Oh yes it started with a bang! <br><br> <b>“What’s your name?” <br>“Doesn’t matter. You’ll forget it once I’m gone.” <br>“No, I won’t.” <br>“I’m Twitch.</b><br><br>*ARC provided by thee awesome author for an honest review*<br><br>Check out my blog for more reviews!<br><br>Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://zakirrahsbookblog.blogspot.co.uk/">http://zakirrahsbookblog.blogspot.co.uk/</a><br>Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Zakirr">https://www.facebook.com/pages/Zakirr</a>...<br>Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/ZBookBlog">https://twitter.com/ZBookBlog</a><br></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer759011212" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2250394203598280171">First of all when I got the message from Belle Aurora about the ARC I flipped my shit because I LOVED Willing Captive. But then there was this list attached to it of all the deplorable things I had to do to get the ARC and well…I did THEM ALL! Just kidding, just numbers one through six, and a little bit of number 12 for good measure. hehe.<br/><br/>Secondly I want to say BRA-fucking-VO to Belle Aurora because this book is NOT a romance and she doesn't pretend that it's one either. It's a love story, just </span>
  <span id="freeText2250394203598280171" style="display:none">First of all when I got the message from Belle Aurora about the ARC I flipped my shit because I LOVED Willing Captive. But then there was this list attached to it of all the deplorable things I had to do to get the ARC and well…I did THEM ALL! Just kidding, just numbers one through six, and a little bit of number 12 for good measure. hehe.<br /><br />Secondly I want to say BRA-fucking-VO to Belle Aurora because this book is NOT a romance and she doesn't pretend that it's one either. It's a love story, just not the kind with an HEA, so DO NOT EXPECT ONE. She makes no apologies, it's just the way the story needed to be told, and she does a hell of a great job of telling it. <br /><br />I have a confession. I LOVE TWITCH. Like Super Love Twitch. I know the author has no plans on a sequel, but I would like some MORE TWITCH. Please and thank you. There hasn't been a character as unique as him in a long while and I could go for Twitch round 2. <br /><br />This book is taring up all the charts and has every reason to be because it really is unique and the writing is solid. I don't like leaving spoilers in my reviews but I will say that there is one moment that had me literally crying and I haven't cried that hard since writing The Dark Light of Day.<br /><br />I don't need to tell you to add it to your TBR cause it's probably already on there. </span>

Can you fucking believe it! A book without gray eyes! LOL! <br><br>I will say this book kept my attention and kept me wanting to know more, even if I didn't wind up completely satisfied with the way everything went down. <br><br>I was a little bit disappointed with Twitch's reasoning for getting Alexa and thought it could have been better developed. <br><br>I also thought there was quite a bit of skipping around and had to reread a few parts since it seemed they were at the club and then all of a sudden she's at home. IDK I guess I just felt there were a few holes.... All in all I still say its worth reading. <br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY/tumblr_inline_mjiydgYd3j1qz4rgp_zpsdd69da0c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_826851333" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/826851333" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/826851333?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940148861119" href="/book/show/18468559-raw">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=frustrating">frustrating</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=bdsm-or-person-in-control">bdsm-or-person-in-control</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=romantica-or-erotica">romantica-or-erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=multiple-pov">multiple-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=dark-or-taboo">dark-or-taboo</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer826851333" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12155849057364543233"><b>2.5 stars</b>. I'm going soft. I can't believe I'm about to give a middling rating strictly based on some sort of connective emotion for a book which my brain is screaming at me to hate.<br/><br/>Honestly, I can't figure it out. The writing was sloppy in places, so many generic terms and nicknames were used, and we even had a TSTL heroine. Any one of these things alone can cause me to 1 star a book, and this time it was as if the "Stacia hates it" trifecta was out in full force.<br/><br/>Yet, here I am, not hating the </span>
  <span id="freeText12155849057364543233" style="display:none"><b>2.5 stars</b>. I'm going soft. I can't believe I'm about to give a middling rating strictly based on some sort of connective emotion for a book which my brain is screaming at me to hate.<br /><br />Honestly, I can't figure it out. The writing was sloppy in places, so many generic terms and nicknames were used, and we even had a TSTL heroine. Any one of these things alone can cause me to 1 star a book, and this time it was as if the "Stacia hates it" trifecta was out in full force.<br /><br />Yet, here I am, not hating the book, even if I was hating on the main character. It was as if she didn't even want to try to consider common sense at all. Do I give her bonus points for knowing that she was part of the problem? I don't know.<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You, my dear, are a stupid ho."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Twitch was a horrible person, but he never claimed to be otherwise. I can get down for reading about characters who are who they are and make no apologies for it, even if what they are is nothing above despicable. At least evil isn't always boring. <br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"The world needs villains too."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><b>What else drove my rating down :</b> It always comes back to the heroine not taking enough time to think things through in her head. Look, I get the notion of acting without thinking. Most of us at one time or another have jumped feet first into a relationship or situation without considering the consequences. But after the initial warm fuzzies wear off, common sense starts kicking in. And if it's not kicking in, someone, somewhere is going to let you know at some point along the way that you are making a huge mistake (that's what friends and family love to do - tell you that your choices are shit). Oh wait, the friends in this story were unable to see what was wrong either. <br /><br /><i>Guess it sucks to be you, Lexi.</i><br /><br />Speaking of the friends - the chapters with Lexi and her friends were boring as hell. Skim, skim, skim.<br /><br />Random complaints : I am not buying that a 6 year old not only knows how to carve a name into a tree, but was able to remember and spell out a long (full) name having only heard it once. My kid is right around this age and yeah...it's not happening.<br /><br />Also, the description of Lexi on coke sounded more like she was doing acid. Just sayin...<br /><br /><b>Why I still kept reading :</b> I wanted to know how this train wreck could possibly turn out. <i>What happens when the stalker with an agenda ends up questioning his own agenda?</i><br /><br />The story itself had something which kept me interested enough to keep reading. The idea was a good one. I was instantly curious about the guy in a hoodie who was watching Lexi, especially after reading the prologue and knowing right away who he was, even when she didn't have a clue. <br /><br />The build to the reveal at the end had me wondering if there was any way this couple could find a way to make it work, which is a point to the good side. I like to be strung along a little like that. <br /><br />I actually thought the ending was a suitable one. It appears some people didn't like how the story wrapped up, but for me, it was a good stopping point. I honestly hope that this DOES NOT turn into an instance where the fans pressure the author for a book 2. The story can't go to a good place from here without getting tedious or repetitive. It's up to us as the reader to imagine what comes next. And I already decided in my head what has happened, so I don't want to be told otherwise that this isn't the case.<br /><br /><b>Who should read this book?</b> Fans of anti-heroes, sociopaths (wait, are there actual fans of sociopaths?), or taboo mind fuck erotica with an emphasis on unconventional romance.<br /><br /><b>Who should not read this book?</b> All of my fellow picky reader friends. <i>You</i> know who you are. Normally, I'd be on board with all of you in slamming the cliches present here, but I somehow found myself drawn in to the story in spite of the normal annoyance factors.<br /><br />Okay, I'm officially getting off the taboo contemporary book train for a little while. It's been a weird ride this week. I'm ready to go back to the land of something else for the time being.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12155849057364543233" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText10295182753224194776" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>Re-read: 02.11.2016</u>

Twitch still does something to my obvious sick heart and while Alexa still annoys me at time, I don't mind her so much because Twitch makes up for it. The story is still sick, devastation, sexy and raw. And wild, even the second time around reading it. I'm also very sure I'll re-read this yet again in the future. Though after hearing a bit about book #2 in this series, I'm not <i>feeling</i> it to continue the series...cuz I only want Twitch.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He thinks of everybody as nobody. If you don’t give up on him, he’ll make you somebody.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (Adult) Contemporary (Dark) Romance<br><b>Series</b>: - Series (Trilogy?), Book One <br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Twitch. <br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Yes.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Yes.<br><b>Rating</b> - 4 *sick is what I am* stars.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>First read review:</b> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Monsters don't always lurk in the shadows. Sometimes they hide in plain sight.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><i>My casting:</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402962060i/10019619.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You can push a person to change, but the only time the change will stick is when it's something they want to achieve on their own.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>This is probably one of the weirdest and strangest, yet good book that I have ever read. The ending had me crying like a little baby who just lost her puppy!! I sincerely hope that Bella Aurora will be nice to us and write more.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411026071ra/11184953.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“This body is mine to do with what I want. And if you’re good, I’ll make you come. If you’re bad, I’ll leave you hanging. In saying that, I know you’re going to be a good girl. Because you definitely don’t want to disappoint me. Do you, Lexi?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>You're probably wondering why I only gave this book 4/3 stars, and to be honest, this book was a bit to crazy for me. Though, I loved some parts of the book, I still couldn't love the whole part. It was probably too 'raw' for me :P Hehe. But I do recommend people to read this because it's something 'completely out of character, mind blowing and crazy shit' kind of book. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Sometimes good people have to do bad things. It’s nothing personal. It’s just life,”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>When I started reading this book, I did not expect this.. Let's just say that I got one hell of a surprise and do I regret it? HELL NO! I'm sure that in the future I will re-read this awesome book with these awesome, yet scary characters :)!<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Not everyone can be a fairy-tale hero.” He pauses a moment, then adds, “The world needs villains too.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>This book left me feeling dirty but also kinda hot and wet.. so I guess I should just stop writing and just end it with: I really liked the book, but sometimes it was too much for me.<br><b>Rate: 4/3 *shocking, what the hell did i just read?!* stars.</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16984152149577631813"><b>"I’m so ashamed of myself for wanting this. His brand of sex comes with a warning label. That should make me want to run in the opposite direction.-Lexi"</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414381654i/11646961._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Raw is one sexy and dirty read! We have a sweet heroine who has overcome a challenging childhood. Lexi has devoted her life to helping others. As a case worker, she hands out love and strength like air. She has good friends and a good life. She also has a stalker.<br/><br/>Twitch is hard, plays things dirty, and lives life on the wild side. He too has suf</span>
  <span id="freeText16984152149577631813" style="display:none"><b>"I’m so ashamed of myself for wanting this. His brand of sex comes with a warning label. That should make me want to run in the opposite direction.-Lexi"</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414381654i/11646961._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Raw is one sexy and dirty read! We have a sweet heroine who has overcome a challenging childhood. Lexi has devoted her life to helping others. As a case worker, she hands out love and strength like air. She has good friends and a good life. She also has a stalker.<br><br>Twitch is hard, plays things dirty, and lives life on the wild side. He too has suffered through a difficult childhood. He has a secret. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[He is stalking Lexi because she helped him once as a child. He has a messed up belief that because Lexi tried to show him goodness and his life was not good...she should suffer. <b>"You need her. Just her. Nothing else. Ignoring my mind’s voice, I look at my prey. She’s the reason I am the way I am. It’s all her fault. And she’s going to pay."-Twitch </b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> He wants Lexi. He wants to play with her like a dog and a new toy! There is only one problem that Twitch hasn't prepared for...he falls in love with Lexi. <br><br><b>"Running a hand down my face, I think long and hard about what needs to be done, all the while knowing I won’t ever let her go."-Twitch</b><br><br>When Lexi is with Twitch, she forgets everything about being good. She is reckless and free and she loves it! Twitch begins to see Lexi as a part of him. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414381654i/11646962.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Twitch falls hard for Lexi. The sexual chemistry between these two is off the chart. Scandalous and sweet all at once. Lexi and Twitch fall into a comfortable routine. Lexi even helps tame the beast that lives deep within Twitch. Her love begins to heal him.<br><br><b>“ No one touches you. You got that ? As long as I want you, no one else gets you, and after I’m done with you…” He licks my jawline. My eyes flutter. He presses his erection into my thigh. “… you’ll be forever unsatisfied. No one will ever take care of you the way I can. The way I know you want it. I know what you need, Lexi, even if you don’t know it yourself. But I’ll teach you.”-Twitch</b><br><br>Lexi knows that she should walk away. She cannot. She won't. Even when she makes big mistakes. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I was completely dumfounded with how stupid she was. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414382073i/11647002._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Overall, Raw was an excellent read. The emotional development could have been stronger. The characters were obviously physically attracted to one another. I would have liked to have seem a little more emotion from our hero. (I know he is damaged and a super bad ass...but still). Now for the killer of this book. Please do not view this spoiler if you don't want to know what happens. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I was completely devestated that Lexi tells Twitch she is pregnant and then he is killed. But not really killed because the Epilogue jumps ahead five years and he is watching over her. REALLY???? WHAT????? What I really wanted to see in the epilogue is something like this.....<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414381975i/11646981.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> And what is the hardest pill to swallow? We don't know if there will be a follow up. <br><br>After reading raw....you will need to hit this:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414205466ra/11622864.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and then do a little of this:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414205466ra/11622865.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>What is the moral of this review:<br>1) I love bad boys<br>2) I love strong heroines<br>3) I love HEA.....and when I don't get one I feel like this:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414205466ra/11622866.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>And yet, this book was fabulous! I would totally recommend it! </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer810693055" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer6191420302241632665">4.5 Hot Hooded stars...<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388887126i/7950037._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>“There’s something about Twitch. He’s just…raw. Everything about him is raw. And gritty. And unbound. He’s a raging fire. And I’m a fragile moth fluttering into the flame. Sooner or later, I’m going to get burned. I know this. Will I even survive the heat? How can I trust this man after everything we’ve been through in such a short time?”</b><br/><br/>Well get me on the Belle bandwagon, this is the first book I have read by this author and <u>I LOVED IT!</u><br/><br/>This was a nonstop addictive read. O</span>
  <span id="freeText6191420302241632665" style="display:none">4.5 Hot Hooded stars...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388887126i/7950037._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>“There’s something about Twitch. He’s just…raw. Everything about him is raw. And gritty. And unbound. He’s a raging fire. And I’m a fragile moth fluttering into the flame. Sooner or later, I’m going to get burned. I know this. Will I even survive the heat? How can I trust this man after everything we’ve been through in such a short time?”</b><br><br>Well get me on the Belle bandwagon, this is the first book I have read by this author and <u>I LOVED IT!</u><br><br>This was a nonstop addictive read. One I relished and read in a calculative way as to not miss any piece of Lexi and Twitch's story. I loved both MC’s as well as the secondary characters. They all had unique, interesting, flawed, loveable, damaged characteristics allowing me to get enough of them to want more. Some I will not soon forget and some I hope to read more about *hint… to the author.<br><br>Even though I sort of knew where the story was going, I enjoyed the entire journey and I especially enjoyed the relationship development between Lexi and Twitch as well as the melting of his cold Grinch-like heart.<br><br>I think the ending was perfectly selfless and was so fitting for Lexi and Twitch. I know many readers are enraged and shocked, but I thought it was primo. It is best to not read any reviews with spoilers. I had no idea how it would end and I liked it that way.<br><br><u>Some lasting moments:</u><br><br><b>“I’ve never been with a man who has a piercing before. The bar goes vertically, with one silver ball resting on the sensitive underside, and the other just where the head starts on the top of his shaft. He’s thick. He’s long. He’s smooth. He’s impressive.“</b><br><br><b>“If you promise to never leave me, I will love you. And be good to you. I’ll treat you like a queen.”</b><br><br><b>“I don’t like labels. I won’t be defined by words like normal, unbalanced, or damaged. There’s so much more to me than words. I have layers, just like the next person, and if you picked me apart layer-by-layer, you’d find a blackened crust where my heart should be. But ever since Lexi came into my life, a thin bud of greenery sprouted there, giving me hope that even I could be the person who makes someone’s day better.”</b><br><br><br> <br></span>

<div id="review_717799818" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/717799818" />
    <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time"><img alt="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460037460p2/9072385.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/717799818?book_show_action=true">Sep 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="user" itemprop="url" name="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time">*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940148861119" href="/book/show/18468559-raw">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=love">love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=scorching-hot">scorching-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=who-cut-the-cheese">who-cut-the-cheese</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer717799818" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3513358383741213346">4--<b>Twitchy</b>--Stars!!!<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"There's something about Twitch.<br/>He's just....raw.<br/>Everything about him is raw. And gritty. And unbound.<br/>He's a raging fire. And I'm a fragile moth fluttering into the flame. Sooner or later, I'm going to get burned. I know this."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Well call me crazy but I liked this one.....a lot. I'm a <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6983012.Belle_Aurora' title='Belle Aurora' rel='nofollow noopener'>Belle Aurora</a> fan--I've read all of her books. There's just something quirky and different about her writing and her stories. That's what Raw was for me--quirky and different....much like Willi</span>
  <span id="freeText3513358383741213346" style="display:none">4--<b>Twitchy</b>--Stars!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>"There's something about Twitch.<br>He's just....raw.<br>Everything about him is raw. And gritty. And unbound.<br>He's a raging fire. And I'm a fragile moth fluttering into the flame. Sooner or later, I'm going to get burned. I know this."</i>
</b><br><br>Well call me crazy but I liked this one.....a lot. I'm a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6983012.Belle_Aurora" title="Belle Aurora" rel="nofollow noopener">Belle Aurora</a> fan--I've read all of her books. There's just something quirky and different about her writing and her stories. That's what Raw was for me--quirky and different....much like Willing Captive. I didn't think this was a dark read....was it even supposed to be??<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388895804ra/7951861.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It was <b>raw</b> and gritty I suppose but I still found some of the banter and dialogue funny and even cheesy at times. IDK...for me this one seemed to get hyped as some dark, twisted, mind fuckery of a tale but it wasn't like that for me. I just took it for what it was and ended up enjoying it in the process. <br><br>Half of the time I was like <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/242673.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The other half I was trying to decide if I even liked Twitch.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384754880ra/6955745.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I liked the stalker turned lover theme<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385951277ra/7264226.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>....that was something new and different. <br><br>It was apparent from the get-go who Twitch was and his connection to Lexi. It was just a matter of it all playing out....what Twitch's motivation was, etc.<br><br>There were some definite huh moments.....especially<br><br>(1) Finding out Twitch <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[hired the guy to rape/attack Lexi <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>?????<br><br>I didn't get that....at all. His motivation for "going after" Lexi was LAME and <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388895889ra/7951867.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>(2) I kind of find it hard to believe that someone would have a stalker...know they have a stalker....and yet never do anything or tell anyone about it??? Never really question who he is, what he does, etc.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388896027ra/7951870.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>(3) I found Twitch's dominance/control issues in the bedroom more awkward than anything. The belt collar thing...IDK. Don't get me wrong the sex was HOT and dirty but I liked them more together as a "normal" couple. <br><br>Yes, Twitch I used a label...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388040334ra/7727015.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall though I enjoyed the story, the quirkiness of it and the humor in the dialogue. I really liked Lexi's friends Nikki and Dave...they made me lol. <br><br>Even Nox and Lily made an appearance. <br><br>Now for the ending.....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388896427ra/7951942.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Eh....I guess after all of the hype I was expecting something shocking so when it rolled around it was rather anti-climatic for me. It would appear that there may or may not be more books....IDK. I wouldn't be upset either way. I wasn't torn up by the ending.<br><br>Bottom line, I think if you are a fan of Belle Aurora and have read and liked her other books, especially Willing Captive, I think you will like this one. </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="3513358383741213346" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer768819553" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14405754547627251047">Not going to rate it as I did not finish and read enough spoilers from reviews that I am glad I did not finish. On another day, it might have worked for me but not this time.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_818549707" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/818549707" />
    <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog"><img alt="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518242765p2/14302918.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/818549707?book_show_action=true">Jan 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940148861119" href="/book/show/18468559-raw">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=hot-alpha-male">hot-alpha-male</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=guy-is-a-douchebag-but-i-love-him">guy-is-a-douchebag-but-i-love-him</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer818549707" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16020570282691307021">4 Dirty Loving Stars!!<br/>(BR with Melissa)<br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps45dc8754.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390720482i/8269831._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo image_zps45dc8754.jpg' height='400' width='275' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>"Raw" is definitely in a class all its own.<br/>I've never gone back and forth between hating and loving the male lead in a story, ever.<br/><br/>This is not your typical love story.<br/>I felt both characters were extremely flawed and I haven't yet read a story where a woman falls in love with her stalker...till now.<br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps2f3801bb.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390720482i/8269832._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo image_zps2f3801bb.jpg' height='400' width='275' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Twitch and Lexi come from rough childhoods.<br/>They take different paths in life.<br/>Lexi stays on the straight and narrow.<br/>Goes off to College and is working at h</span>
  <span id="freeText16020570282691307021" style="display:none">4 Dirty Loving Stars!!<br>(BR with Melissa)<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps45dc8754.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390720482i/8269831._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps45dc8754.jpg" height="400" width="275" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>"Raw" is definitely in a class all its own.<br>I've never gone back and forth between hating and loving the male lead in a story, ever.<br><br>This is not your typical love story.<br>I felt both characters were extremely flawed and I haven't yet read a story where a woman falls in love with her stalker...till now.<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps2f3801bb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390720482i/8269832._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps2f3801bb.jpg" height="400" width="275" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Twitch and Lexi come from rough childhoods.<br>They take different paths in life.<br>Lexi stays on the straight and narrow.<br>Goes off to College and is working at her dream job, helping children living in foster care.<br>Twitch spent time in Juvi when he was younger and turned to a life of crime which has made him considerably wealthy and powerful.<br><br>The two cross paths because Twitch has been stalking Lexi.<br>An incident occurs which unites them.<br>It only takes a few days before these two are having hot, crazy, and dirty sex!!<br><br><i>
  <b>"There's only one way I fuck. Dirty."</b>
</i> - Twitch<br><br><b>I feel dirty, used, and abused. And I've never felt better.</b> - Lexi<br><br>I questioned a lot of Lexi's decisions and actions.<br>I mean after what she went through, I just couldn't believe she was already willing to have raunchy sex with a complete stranger!<br>And she kept making really fucked up decisions.<br>I pretty much thought she was a bit nuts.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/tumblr_mpdxq7MhF91rzianao1_400_zps0c20f827.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390720482ra/8269833.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mpdxq7MhF91rzianao1_400_zps0c20f827.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I wasn't sure how to take Twitch in the beginning. <br>He was, after all, stalking Lexi for quite some time.<br>I knew right away who he was but couldn't understand why he had some hostility towards Lexi.<br><br>He was so brutal and I get it that he had a condition but sometimes I found it hard to like him.<br>And yet, I did end up really loving Twitch.<br><br>There were quite a few WTF moments in this story.<br>The one at about the 80% mark had my head in a tizzy.<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/20120105031603Wtf_zps33d0387d.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390720483ra/8269834.gif" alt=" photo 20120105031603Wtf_zps33d0387d.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I was about to really HATE this book but luckily things are explained.<br><br>I wasn't a fan of the belt till much later on in the story and I really did love the moments that Twitch showed Lexi his softer side.<br>Those parts made my heart melt for him.<br>I rooted for these two to have their HEA.<br>If any two people deserved it, I'd say it would be them!!<br><br>Again, I have to say I didn't see that ending coming!!<br>The book leaves off in a way that leads me to believe there will be a book 2.<br><br>Hoping that there is a book two!!!!<br><br><br><br><i>
  <b>"The thing is, I'm selfish. And I don't give a fuck about what I deserve. All I care about is what I want. And I want you so fuckin' bad that I'd do almost anything to keep you."</b>
</i><br><br><br><b>There's something about Twitch. He's just...raw. Everything about him is raw. And gritty. And unbound. He's a raging fire. And I'm a fragile moth fluttering into the flame. Sooner or later, I'm going to get burned. I know this.</b><br><br><br><i>
  <b>"You're what fills the hole in my heart."</b>
</i> - Lexi<br><br><br><i>
  <b>"You said you'd never leave me. And I'm holding you to that. Because when you're safe again, I'm coming for you, Angel."</b>
</i><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="16020570282691307021" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1593828028" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1593828028" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1593828028?book_show_action=true">Mar 29, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=crime-mafia">crime-mafia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=2contemporary-lovestories">2contemporary-lovestories</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1593828028" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14018778373764926016"><b>This is not a love story. </b><br/><br/>I love books that illustrate a really good borderline-psychopath stalker. <br/>Twitch is the perfect example. He is not the cute type of stalker. He is a criminal, with a dirty soul. The worst kind. For some reason he blames Lexi for anything bad that has happen to him since he was a child. And when the time comes, Lexi has to pay. Lexi has to be broken.<br/><br/> <blockquote>
  <i>You feeling uncomfortable?” I immediately nod. Squeezing my ass once more, he places his lips at the shell of my ear. “</i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText14018778373764926016" style="display:none"><b>This is not a love story. </b><br /><br />I love books that illustrate a really good borderline-psychopath stalker. <br />Twitch is the perfect example. He is not the cute type of stalker. He is a criminal, with a dirty soul. The worst kind. For some reason he blames Lexi for anything bad that has happen to him since he was a child. And when the time comes, Lexi has to pay. Lexi has to be broken.<br /><br /> <blockquote>
  <i>You feeling uncomfortable?” I immediately nod. Squeezing my ass once more, he places his lips at the shell of my ear. “Good. Get used to it. Because I’m going to do bad things to you.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />Twitch and Lexi’s love story is purely complicated, heartbreaking and breathtaking. <br />They know they are bad for each other and they cannot be apart.<br /><br /> <blockquote>
  <i>“There's something about Twitch.<br />He's just...raw. Everything about him is raw. And gritty. And unbound.<br />He's a raging fire. And I'm a fragile moth fluttering into the flame. Sooner or later, I'm going to get burned. I know this. Will I even survive the heat?”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />And<br /><br /> <blockquote>
  <i>“I need to walk away from you.”<br />His nose runs up the length of mine and my eyes flutter closed. His bottom lip barely touches my top one as he whispers back, “What makes you think I’ll let you, Alexa?”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />And<br /><br /> <blockquote>
  <i>“Walking away, I mentally hear glass cracking under my feet because I step right over my shattered heart.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />This is not a story with a happy ending. I cried my eyes out. It has an ending that breaks your heart and makes you crave for more.<br /><br />I LOVED, LOVED this book.<br />It is dirty, raw, sick, devastating, crazy, dark, just wrong.<br /><br /><br />(I gave 4 stars instead of 5, because I believe that some of the BDSM references in the book were completely irrelevant and unnecessary)</span>
  <a data-text-id="14018778373764926016" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('V/t1LLQXPa+z/oBhxD2cRITVhZ4KjlTpfyNk9dpL7kht3Rz+D0n0xxTVNAAzyJabUopiVsQD2o4kXSJEFwgc0g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ASYWZtNOKQA3LzrmT0HdUBz/0O6gEqZ2bXSoEK/P7AY7AH+0aBDgaJAEjoe4tNePyqA3Jm6fKBE2Cu6hYowenA==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer9242696856406232203">Belle Aurora is thirty-something year old and was born in the land down under. <br/>At an early age she fell in love with reading. Boredom one summer had her scouring the bookshelves at home.   <span id="freeText9242696856406232203" style="display:none">Belle Aurora is thirty-something year old and was born in the land down under. <br />At an early age she fell in love with reading. Boredom one summer had her scouring the bookshelves at home. She stumbled across Sandra Brown’s Breath of Scandal and fell in love with romance.<br />Having been brought up in a loud and boisterous family of Croatian descent, she developed a natural love for dramatics and laughter. Only some years ago had she discovered a new love. <br />Humorous romance novels.<br />So many authors had opened a brand new world where she could lose herself yet feel safe and at home in their stories. Belle has been known to become a screeching banshee while anxiously awaiting their newest titles.<br />Belle never thought she would write. It had never interested her until recently. Friend-Zoned began to form and in February this year Belle typed the words Chapter One. And she fell in love.<br />With words.<br />With writing.<br />With a creative imagination she never knew she harbored.<br /><br />Belle Aurora is a USA Today best-selling author.</span>
